We provided a diverse dataset comprising 100 training, 50 validation, and 50 testing scans collected from multiple international sites (UK, Singapore, and China) with varying MRI protocols and demographics. All annotations followed the STRIVE protocol to ensure standardized ground truth and covered the full brain parenchyma. Seven teams completed the full challenge, implementing various deep learning approaches primarily based on U-Net architectures with innovations in multi-modal processing, ensemble strategies, and transformer-based components. Performance was evaluated using dice similarity coefficient, absolute volume difference, recall, and precision metrics. The winning method employed MedNeXt architecture with a dual 2D/3D strategy for handling varying slice thicknesses. The top solutions showed relatively good performance on test data from seen datasets, but significant degradation of performance was observed on the previously unseen Shanghai cohort, highlighting cross-site generalization challenges due to domain shift. This challenge establishes an important benchmark for EPVS segmentation methods and underscores the need for the continued development of robust algorithms that can generalize in diverse clinical settings.

## 统计金融(q-fin.ST:Statistical Finance)

【1】Reinforcement Learning for Monetary Policy Under Macroeconomic Uncertainty: Analyzing Tabular and Function Approximation Methods
- **标题**: 宏观经济不确定性下货币政策的强化学习：分析表格和函数逼近方法
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.17929
> **作者**: Sheryl Chen,Tony Wang,Kyle Feinstein
> **摘要**: 我们研究当宏观经济关系不确定且随时间变化时，央行应如何动态设定短期名义利率以稳定通胀和失业。我们将货币政策建模为一个顺序决策问题，其中央行每季度观察宏观经济状况并选择利率调整。使用公开的历史美联储经济数据（FRED），我们构建了一个线性高斯转换模型，并实现了具有二次损失奖励函数的离散动作马尔可夫决策过程。我们选择根据泰勒规则和朴素基线来比较九种不同的强化学习风格方法，包括表格 Q 学习变体、SARSA、Actor-Critic、深度 Q 网络、具有不确定性量化的贝叶斯 Q 学习以及具有部分可观测性的 POMDP 公式。令人惊讶的是，标准表格 Q 学习取得了最佳性能（-615.13 +- 309.58 平均回报），优于增强型 RL 方法和传统策略规则。我们的结果表明，虽然复杂的强化学习技术在货币政策应用中显示出希望，但更简单的方法在该领域可能更稳健，这突显了将现代强化学习应用于宏观经济政策的重要挑战。
> **Abstract**: We study how a central bank should dynamically set short-term nominal interest rates to stabilize inflation and unemployment when macroeconomic relationships are uncertain and time-varying. We model monetary policy as a sequential decision-making problem where the central bank observes macroeconomic conditions quarterly and chooses interest rate adjustments. Using publically accessible historical Federal Reserve Economic Data (FRED), we construct a linear-Gaussian transition model and implement a discrete-action Markov Decision Process with a quadratic loss reward function. We chose to compare nine different reinforcement learning style approaches against Taylor Rule and naive baselines, including tabular Q-learning variants, SARSA, Actor-Critic, Deep Q-Networks, Bayesian Q-learning with uncertainty quantification, and POMDP formulations with partial observability. Surprisingly, standard tabular Q-learning achieved the best performance (-615.13 +- 309.58 mean return), outperforming both enhanced RL methods and traditional policy rules. Our results suggest that while sophisticated RL techniques show promise for monetary policy applications, simpler approaches may be more robust in this domain, highlighting important challenges in applying modern RL to macroeconomic policy.

【2】Inferring Latent Market Forces: Evaluating LLM Detection of Gamma Exposure Patterns via Obfuscation Testing
- **标题**: 推断潜在市场力量：通过混淆测试评估 LLM 对伽马暴露模式的检测
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.17923
> **作者**: Christopher Regan,Ying Xie
> **摘要**: 我们引入了混淆测试，这是一种新颖的方法，用于验证大型语言模型是否通过因果推理而不是时间关联来检测结构市场模式。在标准普尔 500 指数期权数据的 242 个交易日（95.6% 覆盖率）上测试三种交易商对冲约束模式（伽玛定位、股票锁定、0DTE 对冲）时，我们发现法学硕士使用无偏提示实现了 71.5% 的检测率，该提示仅提供原始伽玛暴露值，没有制度标签或时间背景。 WHO-WHOM-WHAT 因果框架迫使模型识别经济参与者（交易商）、受影响方（定向交易者）以及观察到的市场动态背后的结构机制（强制对冲）。至关重要的是，即使经济盈利能力按季度变化，检测准确性 (91.2%) 仍然保持稳定，这表明模型识别结构性约束而不是盈利模式。当提示使用制度标签时，检测率增加到 100%，但 71.5% 的无偏率验证了真正的模式识别。我们的研究结果表明，法学硕士拥有通过纯粹的结构推理来检测复杂金融机制的新兴能力，这对系统战略开发、风险管理以及我​​们对变压器架构如何处理金融市场动态的理解具有影响。
> **Abstract**: We introduce obfuscation testing, a novel methodology for validating whether large language models detect structural market patterns through causal reasoning rather than temporal association. Testing three dealer hedging constraint patterns (gamma positioning, stock pinning, 0DTE hedging) on 242 trading days (95.6% coverage) of S&P 500 options data, we find LLMs achieve 71.5% detection rate using unbiased prompts that provide only raw gamma exposure values without regime labels or temporal context. The WHO-WHOM-WHAT causal framework forces models to identify the economic actors (dealers), affected parties (directional traders), and structural mechanisms (forced hedging) underlying observed market dynamics. Critically, detection accuracy (91.2%) remains stable even as economic profitability varies quarterly, demonstrating that models identify structural constraints rather than profitable patterns. When prompted with regime labels, detection increases to 100%, but the 71.5% unbiased rate validates genuine pattern recognition. Our findings suggest LLMs possess emergent capabilities for detecting complex financial mechanisms through pure structural reasoning, with implications for systematic strategy development, risk management, and our understanding of how transformer architectures process financial market dynamics.

## 量子物理学(quant-ph:Quantum Physics)

【1】Sonified Quantum Seizures. Sonification of time series in epileptic seizures and simulation of seizures via quantum modelling
- **标题**: 声化量子癫痫。癫痫发作时间序列的声音化和通过量子建模模拟癫痫发作
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.19272
> **作者**: Maria Mannone,Paulo Vitor Itaborai,Omar Costa Hamido,Miriam Goldack,Norbert Marwan,Peppino Fazio,Patrizia Ribino
> **摘要**: 我们应用可听化策略和量子计算来分析癫痫发作。我们首先对来自选定通道（来自真实 ECoG 数据）的信号进行声音化，获得复调序列。然后，我们提出了两种量子方法来模拟类似的癫痫发作，并对结果进行声音化。声音的比较可以提示真实数据和模拟之间的相似性和差异，有助于完善 \textit{in silico} 模型。这是一种开创性的方法，展示了量子计算和声化技术的结合如何拓宽真实数据调查的视角，并帮助定义用于分析和预测癫痫发作的新测试平台。
> **Abstract**: We apply sonification strategies and quantum computing to the analysis of an episode of seizure. We first sonify the signal from a selection of channels (from real ECoG data), obtaining a polyphonic sequence. Then, we propose two quantum approaches to simulate a similar episode of seizure, and we sonify the results. The comparison of sonifications can give hints on similarities and discrepancies between real data and simulations, helping refine the \textit{in silico} model. This is a pioneering approach, showing how the combination of quantum computing and sonification can broaden the perspective of real-data investigation, and helping define a new test bench for analysis and prediction of seizures.

【2】Multifractality Analysis of Single Qubit Quantum Circuit Outcomes for a Superconducting Quantum Computer
- **标题**: 超导量子计算机的单量子位量子电路结果的多重分形分析
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.18491
> **作者**: Mohammadreza Saghafi,Lamine Mili,Karlton Wirsing
> **摘要**: 我们对在 IBM 超导量子计算机上重复运行单量子位量子电路获得的时间序列数据进行了多重分形分析，其中测量结果记录为零的数量。通过应用先进的信号处理技术，包括小波前导方法和多重分形去趋势波动分析，我们发现了输出数据中强烈的多重分形行为。这一发现表明，量子电路输出固有的时间波动并不是纯粹随机的，而是在多个时间尺度上表现出复杂的缩放特性。信号的多重分形性质表明可以定制专门针对这些缩放特征的滤波策略，以有效减轻量子计算中的噪声。我们的结果不仅有助于更深入地了解重复测量下量子系统的动力学特性，而且还为改进近期量子器件中的降噪技术提供了一条有前途的途径。
> **Abstract**: We present a multifractal analysis of time series data obtained by repeatedly running a single-qubit quantum circuit on IBM superconducting quantum computers, in which the measurement outcomes are recorded as the number of zeros. By applying advanced signal processing techniques, including the wavelet leader method and multifractal detrended fluctuation analysis, we uncover strong multifractal behavior in the output data. This finding indicates that the temporal fluctuations inherent to quantum circuit outputs are not purely random but exhibit complex scaling properties across multiple time scales. The multifractal nature of the signal suggests the possibility of tailoring filtering strategies that specifically target these scaling features to effectively mitigate noise in quantum computations. Our results not only contribute to a deeper understanding of the dynamical properties of quantum systems under repeated measurement but also provide a promising avenue for improving noise reduction techniques in near-term quantum devices.

【3】Evolutionary BP+OSD Decoding for Low-Latency Quantum Error Correction
- **标题**: 用于低延迟量子纠错的进化 BP+OSD 解码
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.18273
> **作者**: Hee-Youl Kwak,Seong-Joon Park,Hyunwoo Jung,Jeongseok Ha,Jae-Won Kim
> **摘要**: 我们提出了一种用于量子纠错的进化信念传播（EBP）解码器，它将可训练的权重纳入BP算法中，并通过差分进化算法对其进行优化。这种方法可以结合有序统计解码 (OSD) 来实现 EBP 的端到端优化。表面码和量子低密度奇偶校验码的实验结果表明，EBP+OSD 比 BP+OSD 实现了更好的解码性能和更低的计算复杂度，特别是在严格的低延迟约束下（5 次 BP 迭代内）。
> **Abstract**: We propose an evolutionary belief propagation (EBP) decoder for quantum error correction, which incorporates trainable weights into the BP algorithm and optimizes them via the differential evolution algorithm. This approach enables end-to-end optimization of the EBP combined with ordered statistics decoding (OSD). Experimental results on surface codes and quantum low-density parity-check codes show that EBP+OSD achieves better decoding performance and lower computational complexity than BP+OSD, particularly under strict low latency constraints (within 5 BP iterations).

【4】Shuttling Compiler for Trapped-Ion Quantum Computers Based on Large Language Models
- **标题**: 基于大语言模型的俘获离子量子计算机穿梭编译器
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.18021
> **作者**: Fabian Kreppel,Reza Salkhordeh,Ferdinand Schmidt-Kaler,André Brinkmann
> **摘要**: 基于分段陷阱的俘获离子量子计算机依靠穿梭操作在量子处理单元内的多个子寄存器之间建立连接。几种复杂性不断增加的架构已经被实现，包括线性阵列、跑道环路和基于连接点的布局。随着硬件功能的进步，控制堆栈中需要灵活的软件层来管理量子位路由$\unicode{x2014}$动态重新配置量子位位置的过程，以便参与门操作的所有量子位都位于同一段内。现有方法通常采用特定于体系结构的启发式方法，随着系统复杂性的增加，这种方法变得不切实际。为了应对这一挑战，我们提出了一种基于大语言模型（LLM）的布局独立编译策略。具体来说，我们对预训练的 LLM 进行微调以生成所需的穿梭操作。我们在线性和分支一维架构上评估了这种方法，证明它为开发用于捕获离子量子计算机的基于 LLM 的穿梭编译器提供了基础。
> **Abstract**: Trapped-ion quantum computers based on segmented traps rely on shuttling operations to establish connectivity between multiple sub-registers within a quantum processing unit. Several architectures of increasing complexity have already been realized, including linear arrays, racetrack loops, and junction-based layouts. As hardware capabilities advance, the need arises for flexible software layers within the control stack to manage qubit routing$\unicode{x2014}$the process of dynamically reconfiguring qubit positions so that all qubits involved in a gate operation are co-located within the same segment. Existing approaches typically employ architecture-specific heuristics, which become impractical as system complexity grows. To address this challenge, we propose a layout-independent compilation strategy based on large language models (LLMs). Specifically, we fine-tune pretrained LLMs to generate the required shuttling operations. We evaluate this approach on both linear and branched one-dimensional architectures, demonstrating that it provides a foundation for developing LLM-based shuttling compilers for trapped-ion quantum computers.

## 计算(stat.CO:Computation)

【1】A Critical Review of Monte Carlo Algorithms Balancing Performance and Probabilistic Accuracy with AI Augmented Framework
- **标题**: 使用人工智能增强框架平衡性能和概率准确性的蒙特卡罗算法的批判性评论
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.17968
> **作者**: Ravi Prasad
> **摘要**: 蒙特卡罗算法是现代计算科学的基础支柱，但其有效应用取决于对其性能权衡的深入理解。本文对蒙特卡罗算法的演变进行了批判性分析，重点关注统计效率和计算成本之间持续存在的紧张关系。我们描述了从基本的 Metropolis Hastings 算法到汉密尔顿蒙特卡罗等现代方法的历史发展。这项调查的重点是对时间和空间复杂性的严格讨论，包括每个主要算法类别的上限、下限和渐近紧界。我们研究了开发这些方法的具体动机以及关键的理论和实践观察，例如在 HMC 中引入梯度信息和自适应调整，从而相继产生更好的解决方案。此外，我们提供了一个论证框架，讨论了对于同一问题使用一种算法明显优于另一种算法的明确情况。本文最后评估了这些算法的深远意义和影响，并详细介绍了当前的主要研究挑战。
> **Abstract**: Monte Carlo algorithms are a foundational pillar of modern computational science, yet their effective application hinges on a deep understanding of their performance trade offs. This paper presents a critical analysis of the evolution of Monte Carlo algorithms, focusing on the persistent tension between statistical efficiency and computational cost. We describe the historical development from the foundational Metropolis Hastings algorithm to contemporary methods like Hamiltonian Monte Carlo. A central emphasis of this survey is the rigorous discussion of time and space complexity, including upper, lower, and asymptotic tight bounds for each major algorithm class. We examine the specific motivations for developing these methods and the key theoretical and practical observations such as the introduction of gradient information and adaptive tuning in HMC that led to successively better solutions. Furthermore, we provide a justification framework that discusses explicit situations in which using one algorithm is demonstrably superior to another for the same problem. The paper concludes by assessing the profound significance and impact of these algorithms and detailing major current research challenges.

## 方法论(stat.ME:Methodology)

【1】The Illusion of Consistency: Selection-Induced Bias in Gated Kalman Innovation Statistics
- **标题**: 一致性的错觉：门控卡尔曼创新统计中选择引起的偏差
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.18508
> **作者**: Barak Or
> **摘要**: 验证门控是经典的基于卡尔曼的跟踪系统的基本组成部分。只有归一化新息平方 (NIS) 低于规定阈值的测量才会考虑进行状态更新。虽然这一过程在统计上是由卡方分布驱动的，但它隐含地将无条件创新过程替换为有条件观察的过程，仅限于验证事件。本文表明，门控后计算的创新统计数据收敛于门条件量而不是名义量。在经典的线性高斯假设下，我们推导了以椭球门控为条件的新息的一阶和二阶矩的精确表达式，并表明门控会导致新息协方差的确定性、维度相关的收缩。该分析扩展到 NN 关联，它被证明充当附加的统计选择算子。我们证明，在多个门内测量中选择最小范数创新会导致不可避免的能量收缩，这意味着名义创新统计数据无法在非平凡的门控和关联下保留。二维情况下的封闭形式结果量化了组合效应并说明了其实际意义。
> **Abstract**: Validation gating is a fundamental component of classical Kalman-based tracking systems. Only measurements whose normalized innovation squared (NIS) falls below a prescribed threshold are considered for state update. While this procedure is statistically motivated by the chi-square distribution, it implicitly replaces the unconditional innovation process with a conditionally observed one, restricted to the validation event. This paper shows that innovation statistics computed after gating converge to gate-conditioned rather than nominal quantities. Under classical linear--Gaussian assumptions, we derive exact expressions for the first- and second-order moments of the innovation conditioned on ellipsoidal gating, and show that gating induces a deterministic, dimension-dependent contraction of the innovation covariance. The analysis is extended to NN association, which is shown to act as an additional statistical selection operator. We prove that selecting the minimum-norm innovation among multiple in-gate measurements introduces an unavoidable energy contraction, implying that nominal innovation statistics cannot be preserved under nontrivial gating and association. Closed-form results in the two-dimensional case quantify the combined effects and illustrate their practical significance.

【2】On Efficient Adjustment in Causal Graphs
- **标题**: 论因果图的有效调整
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.18315
> **作者**: Isabela Belciug,Simon Ferreira,Charles K. Assaad
> **摘要**: 流行病学等领域的观察性研究通常依靠协变量调整来估计因果效应。经典的图形标准，如后门标准和广义调整标准，是识别有向无环图 (DAG) 中有效调整集的强大工具。然而，这些标准并不直接适用于汇总因果图 (SCG)，它是动态系统中常用的 DAG 的抽象。在 SCG 中，每个节点通常代表整个时间序列，并且可能涉及循环，使得经典标准不适用于识别因果效应。最近的工作建立了完整的条件，用于确定治疗或暴露 $X_{t-γ}$ 对结果 $Y_t$ 的微观因果效应是否可以通过 SCG 中的协变量调整来识别，假设没有隐藏的混杂因素。然而，这些可识别性条件有两个主要限制。首先，它们很复杂，依赖于繁琐的定义，并且需要枚举 SCG 中的多个路径，这在计算上可能会很昂贵。其次，当满足这些条件时，它们仅提供两个有效的调整集，限制了实际应用中的灵活性。在本文中，我们提出了这些可识别性条件的等效但更简单的公式，并引入了一种新标准，可以识别 SCG 中更广泛的有效调整集类别。此外，我们还描述了其中的准最优调整集，即最小化因果效应估计量的渐近方差的调整集。我们的贡献提供了理论进步和实用工具，可以在抽象因果图中进行更灵活、更高效的因果推理。
> **Abstract**: Observational studies in fields such as epidemiology often rely on covariate adjustment to estimate causal effects. Classical graphical criteria, like the back-door criterion and the generalized adjustment criterion, are powerful tools for identifying valid adjustment sets in directed acyclic graphs (DAGs). However, these criteria are not directly applicable to summary causal graphs (SCGs), which are abstractions of DAGs commonly used in dynamic systems. In SCGs, each node typically represents an entire time series and may involve cycles, making classical criteria inapplicable for identifying causal effects. Recent work established complete conditions for determining whether the micro causal effect of a treatment or an exposure $X_{t-γ}$ on an outcome $Y_t$ is identifiable via covariate adjustment in SCGs, under the assumption of no hidden confounding. However, these identifiability conditions have two main limitations. First, they are complex, relying on cumbersome definitions and requiring the enumeration of multiple paths in the SCG, which can be computationally expensive. Second, when these conditions are satisfied, they only provide two valid adjustment sets, limiting flexibility in practical applications. In this paper, we propose an equivalent but simpler formulation of those identifiability conditions and introduce a new criterion that identifies a broader class of valid adjustment sets in SCGs. Additionally, we characterize the quasi-optimal adjustment set among these, i.e., the one that minimizes the asymptotic variance of the causal effect estimator. Our contributions offer both theoretical advancement and practical tools for more flexible and efficient causal inference in abstracted causal graphs.
